[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is an **OS Command Injection** vulnerability, classified as a critical [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity issue. The vulnerability allows execution of operating system commands [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith attacker-controlled data, which can lead to remote code execution.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe exception trace reveals the following execution flow:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpackage/archive file[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The `TikaCLI` processes input through its `FileEmbeddedDocumentExtractor`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The `PackageParser` handles package entries and attempts to parse them[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. During the parsing process, a `CompositeDetector` is invoked to detect file [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypes[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method is called, which attempts to execute an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOS command[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method creates a `ProcessBuilder` and starts a new [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocess[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. The Jazzer sanitizer detects that the OS command contains attacker-controlled [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata and raises a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Entry Point**: The issue manifests when processing embedded documents within [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpackage files [0m[1;39m([0m[39marchives, containers, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Detection Point**: The security issue is caught at `[0m[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Jazzer sanitizer, specifically in `[0m[1;35mOsCommandInjection.processImplStartHook[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Vulnerable Component**: The `ShellCodeDetector` class at line [0m[1;36m103[0m[39m in its [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Execution Path**: The vulnerability occurs during automatic file type [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection, which is part of Tika's normal parsing workflow[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtis.getPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, tmpFile, StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:        ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mpb.directory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:            FileProcessResult result = [0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpb, [0m[1;36m20000[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m100000[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mresult.getExitValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mmetadata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mSHELL_NO_ARGS, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m finally [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mFileUtils.deleteDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtmpDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:        return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m111[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m112[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:    private MediaType [0m[1;35misShell[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean isShell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m114[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39misShell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:            return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:        return MediaType.OCTET_STREAM;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m118[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m119[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-core/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org.apache.tika.detect.Detector:[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[39m:org.apache.tika.detect.ShellCodeDetector[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for OS Command Injection Vulnerability in ShellCodeDetector[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Analysis Summary[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability analysis reveals a critical OS Command Injection flaw in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ShellCodeDetector.java`. The detector executes user-controlled files from [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted sources [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike archive entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to determine if they are [0m[32m"no-arg"[0m[39m shell [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscripts. Even though filename sanitization is applied, the fundamental issue is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The **file content** is attacker-controlled [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcopied from the input stream[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The file is **executed as a command** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot passed as an argument to a safe [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. This occurs automatically during normal Tika operations when processing archives[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability chain: Archive Entry ‚Üí Metadata with filename ‚Üí [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mShellCodeDetector.detect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ‚Üí File execution ‚Üí RCE[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights from Code Analysis[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **ShellCodeDetector [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m87[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Attempts to execute shell scripts to test [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif they run without arguments[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Insufficient Sanitization**: Lines [0m[1;36m90[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m91[0m[39m sanitize the filename but cannot [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent malicious file content from being executed[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Safe Patterns Exist**: Other detectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFileCommandDetector, ExternalParser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse the safe pattern of executing known safe executables with user files as escaped[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marguments[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Built-in Exclusion Mechanism**: Tika supports excluding detectors via XML [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration or programmatically[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **SPI Auto-loading**: ShellCodeDetector is registered in [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`META-INF/services/org.apache.tika.detect.Detector`, making it active by default[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe optimal fix is to **disable ShellCodeDetector by default** while preserving [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackward compatibility for users who explicitly need this functionality. This [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequires a multi-layered approach:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove ShellCodeDetector from Default Auto-loading [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrimary Fix[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-core/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org.apache.tika.detect.Detector`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Remove or comment out line [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# org.apache.tika.detect.ShellCodeDetector[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This prevents ShellCodeDetector from being automatically loaded by the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServiceLoader[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users processing untrusted input will no longer be vulnerable by default[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who need this detector can still enable it explicitly via configuration[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Add System Property Guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDefense in Depth[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/detect/ShellCodeDetector.java`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Add a system property check at the beginning of the `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m54[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m@Override[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic MediaType [0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream input, Metadata metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Add security guard - require explicit opt-in via system property[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mBoolean.getBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"tika.detector.shell.enable"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return MediaType.OCTET_STREAM;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Existing logic continues[0m[33m...[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    boolean isShell = false;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    String name = [0m[1;35mmetadata.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaCoreProperties.RESOURCE_NAME_KEY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m rest of the method[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provides defense in depth even if the detector is explicitly enabled[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Requires users to set `-Dtika.detector.shell.[0m[33menable[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` to use this detector[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Makes the security risk explicit and intentional[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not break existing functionality - just requires opt-in[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Add Security Warning Documentation[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/detect/ShellCodeDetector.java`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Action**: Update the class-level Javadoc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m43[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m45[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * Simple detector to determine if a shell script is a no-arg shell script.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <p><strong>SECURITY WARNING:<[0m[35m/[0m[95mstrong[0m[39m> This detector executes shell scripts to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * if they can run without arguments. This poses a <strong>CRITICAL SECURITY [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRISK<[0m[35m/[0m[95mstrong[0m[39m>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * when processing untrusted input, as it can lead to <strong>REMOTE CODE [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEXECUTION<[0m[35m/[0m[95mstrong[0m[39m>.<[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <p>This detector is <strong>DISABLED BY DEFAULT<[0m[35m/[0m[95mstrong[0m[39m> for security reasons. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo enable it,[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * you must:<[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <ol>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *   <li>Set the system property: [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>-Dtika.detector.shell.[0m[33menable[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m><[0m[35m/[0m[95mli[0m[39m>[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *   <li>Explicitly include it in your Tika configuration<[0m[35m/[0m[95mli[0m[39m>[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *   <li>Only process files from <strong>TRUSTED SOURCES<[0m[35m/[0m[95mstrong[0m[39m><[0m[35m/[0m[95mli[0m[39m>[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mol[0m[39m>[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * <p><strong>DO NOT ENABLE THIS DETECTOR<[0m[35m/[0m[95mstrong[0m[39m> when processing files from [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * sources such as user uploads, email attachments, or downloaded files.<[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * @since Apache Tika X.X[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic class ShellCodeDetector implements Detector [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Makes the security implications explicit in the code documentation[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Guides developers on safe usage[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provides clear warning against using with untrusted input[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve Backward Compatibility[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No code changes needed for this aspect**, but ensure:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who explicitly configure ShellCodeDetector in their `tika-config.xml` can [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill use it[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The system property guard allows intentional enabling[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing tests that rely on ShellCodeDetector can set the system property[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Comment out the SPI registration[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-core/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org.apache.tika.detect.Detector`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m: Change `org.apache.tika.detect.ShellCodeDetector` to `# [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morg.apache.tika.detect.ShellCodeDetector`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Add system property guard[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/detect/ShellCodeDetector.java`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Insert the guard check at the beginning of the `[0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Return `MediaType.OCTET_STREAM` if the property is not set[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: Update documentation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `tika-core/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/detect/ShellCodeDetector.java`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the existing Javadoc comment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m43[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m45[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the comprehensive [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity warning[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m**: Update any tests that use ShellCodeDetector[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests should set the system property: [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSystem.setProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"tika.detector.shell.enable"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"true"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures tests continue to work while production code is secure by default[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Strategy is Optimal[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses the Root Cause**: Disables the dangerous detector by default while [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing opt-in[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Only requires commenting out one line and adding a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard check[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: Users who explicitly need this functionality can still [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menable it[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Multiple layers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSPI removal + system property + [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocumentation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Follows Secure by Default Principle**: Safe out of the box, unsafe only when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly enabled[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: No changes to the core detector logic or other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Aligns with Tika Architecture**: Uses existing exclusion mechanisms and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: Users who rely on the SHELL_NO_ARGS metadata property will no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger get this information by default.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is acceptable because the feature provides minimal value compared to the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity risk[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who need this specific functionality can explicitly enable it[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vast majority of Tika users process untrusted input and should not have this [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeature enabled[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: Existing deployments that unknowingly relied on ShellCodeDetector [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill see behavior changes.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is a **security fix**, so behavior changes are acceptable and necessary[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The change prevents RCE vulnerabilities in production systems[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users processing only trusted files can re-enable if needed[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Release notes should clearly document this security fix[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Sandboxing the execution**: Too complex, error-prone, and still risky[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Improved filename sanitization**: Doesn't address the fundamental issue of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecuting user content[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Removing ShellCodeDetector entirely**: Too disruptive for users who might [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimately need it[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Making it configurable but enabled by default**: Defeats the purpose of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecuring by default[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe proposed strategy provides the best balance of security, compatibility, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musability.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report clearly identifies an OS Command Injection vulnerability in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ShellCodeDetector` where untrusted shell scripts are executed during file type [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection. The previous patch attempt correctly identified the solution - adding a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystem property guard to disable execution by default - but failed because it tried[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto modify a service configuration file [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`META-INF/services/org.apache.tika.detect.Detector`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that the patching system [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoesn't recognize as a valid language file.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFrom the code analysis:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause**: Lines [0m[1;36m87[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m[39m of `ShellCodeDetector.java` execute the shell [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscript content to determine if it's a [0m[32m"no-arg"[0m[39m script, creating a critical security[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Safe Detection Logic**: Lines [0m[1;36m54[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m[39m perform safe detection via filename [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextensions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.sh, .bash[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and shebang patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39m#![0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which should be preserved.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Service Configuration**: The attempt to modify [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`META-INF/services/org.apache.tika.detect.Detector` failed because resource files [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcannot be patched. However, this modification is unnecessary - we can disable the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdangerous behavior directly in the Java code.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Existing Patterns**: The codebase shows established patterns for system [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperty-based feature toggles [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mBoolean.getBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"org.apache.tika.service.error.warn"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in ServiceLoader[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Detector Exclusion Mechanism**: While Tika has XML-based detector exclusion [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupport, relying on user configuration for security is unacceptable - the detector [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust be secure by default.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Approach[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify only the `ShellCodeDetector.java` file to add a system property guard that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisables shell script execution by default while preserving safe detection [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapabilities. This is a [0m[32m"secure by default"[0m[39m approach that:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Prevents OS Command Injection vulnerability without requiring user action[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Maintains backward compatibility for shell script detection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mby extension and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshebang[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Provides an opt-in mechanism for users who need the full functionality with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrusted content[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Requires no changes to service configuration files or external resources[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Update Class-Level Javadoc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m45[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEnhance the Javadoc to include comprehensive security warnings:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mark the detector as disabled by default due to critical security risk[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Explain that it executes shell scripts in full mode [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE vulnerability[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Document the default safe behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdetection without execution[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Explain the opt-in mechanism via system property `tika.detector.shell.enable`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provide strong warnings about only using with trusted content[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- List what functionality is available in safe vs. full mode[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Add System Property Guard in [0m[1;35mdetect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInsert a security guard immediately after line [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, before the execution logic [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbegins:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Security guard: Disable execution by default due to critical security risk[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This detector executes shell scripts to test if they run without arguments,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m which allows remote code execution when processing untrusted files.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Set -Dtika.detector.shell.[0m[33menable[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m to enable execution for TRUSTED content [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mBoolean.getBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"tika.detector.shell.enable"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return SHELL_SCRIPT;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why after line [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m?**[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m54[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m[39m perform safe detection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextension check, shebang parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- At line [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, we know: [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m file is detected as shell script, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m we have a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfilename, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m we have input stream[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m87[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m[39m perform dangerous execution - this is what we need to skip by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Returning `SHELL_SCRIPT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot `OCTET_STREAM`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m preserves detection capability and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintains compatibility[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Return Value When Disabled**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReturn `SHELL_SCRIPT` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mMediaType.application[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"x-sh"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than `OCTET_STREAM`:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Preserves shell script detection achieved through safe checks[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains backward compatibility with existing code expecting [0m[32m"application/x-sh"[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Works correctly with `CompositeDetector`'s specialization logic[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only loses the `SHELL_NO_ARGS` metadata property [0m[1;39m([0m[39macceptable trade-off[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### What Gets Preserved[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Shell script detection by extension**: Files ending in .sh or .bash are [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Shell script detection by shebang**: Files starting with #! are detected  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **MediaType return**: Still returns [0m[32m"application/x-sh"[0m[39m for shell scripts[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backward compatibility**: Existing tests and workflows continue to work[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Integration**: Works correctly in detector chains and composite detectors[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### What Gets Disabled [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBy Default[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Shell script execution**: Lines [0m[1;36m87[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m110[0m[39m are skipped when property is not set[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **SHELL_NO_ARGS metadata**: This property will never be set when disabled[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No-arg detection**: Cannot determine if scripts run without arguments[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is acceptable because:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No code dependencies on `SHELL_NO_ARGS` were found in the codebase[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The feature requires dangerous execution that cannot be safely implemented[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who need it can opt-in with full awareness of security implications[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security**: Eliminates OS Command Injection vulnerability by default without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequiring user action[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Compatibility**: Maintains shell script detection capability through safe [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Non-breaking**: Existing code expecting [0m[32m"application/x-sh"[0m[39m continues to work[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Follows patterns**: Uses `[0m[1;35mBoolean.getBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern established in Tika [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., ServiceLoader[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No external dependencies**: Only modifies Java source code, avoiding the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresource file patching issue[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Opt-in available**: Users can enable full functionality for trusted content [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia `-Dtika.detector.shell.[0m[33menable[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Clear documentation**: Enhanced Javadoc provides comprehensive security [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguidance[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why modify only ShellCodeDetector.java:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The service configuration file modification is unnecessary and causes patch [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The detector will still be loaded via ServiceLoader, but will safely decline to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute by default[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. This approach doesn't break the service provider mechanism[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The security fix is self-contained within the vulnerable class[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the evaluation report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Initial issue**: Eliminates OS Command Injection by preventing execution of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted shell scripts[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Additional issue**: Avoids the [0m[32m"Permission denied"[0m[39m error by not attempting to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodify META-INF/services files[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Execution chain**: The vulnerable `[0m[1;35mProcessUtils.execute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call is never [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreached when the system property is not set[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backward compatibility**: Basic shell script detection continues to work, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining existing functionality[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Side effect**: `SHELL_NO_ARGS` property will not be set by default[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: No known dependencies on this property; acceptable loss for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Side effect**: Users needing no-arg detection must set a system property[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Clear documentation in Javadoc explaining the opt-in mechanism[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Side effect**: May affect workflows relying on execution behavior[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: These workflows should be reviewed as they process untrusted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent unsafely; opt-in available for trusted content[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy provides the optimal balance between security, compatibility, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpracticality while following established patterns in the Tika codebase.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
